      <p class="min-height"><b>From the Business:</b>I am a wedding and lifestyle portrait photographer with more than ten years of experience photographing, what I like to call, “life happening.”
I am passionate about capturing celebrations and milestones in people’s lives. Based in the San Francisco Bay Area, I am fortunate to photograph at stunning locations across California and beyond. My photography style is candid, timeless, romantic, and lighthearted, with an editorial influence. My clients often describe my images as sensitive, genuine, intimate, and spontaneous. My affinity for natural light and organic details allows me to incorporate elements of the surrounding environment into my photography—a soft fern blurring into the foreground, or ancient redwoods framing kissing lovers.
In 2003, I photographed my first wedding in the Sierra National Forest for a dear friend. Guests waded through the creek bed with drinks in hand. The bride and groom exchanged promises on a solitary patch of earth. The bride’s father’s eyes welled with tears and her grandmother’s weathered hands held her bouquet for safekeeping. I knew then that the greatest gift I can give others is to capture images of their most precious occasions. As a result, at the core of my philosophy lies my passion for story-telling and capturing moments that cannot be staged.
I believe in true love, laughing out loud, including everyone, living in the moment, small acts of kindness, the magic of simple things, holding hands, traveling to foreign lands, and singing your heart out to your favorite songs.
Your life story is unique. My goal as a photographer is to illustrate who you are, the interesting parts of your relationship, the arch of emotions that build your story, life’s authenticity and the profound experiences that shape who we are.<span class="more-links" style="display: none;"><a title="Read More about Christine Glebov Photography" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDescriptionWeb(this)">Read more</a></span></p>

Based in the sun-kissed landscapes of San Diego, my lens extends its reach to the vibrant communities of San Marcos, Temecula, Menifee, Murrieta, Orange County, and the dynamic energy of Los Angeles.
Photography, for me, is not just a profession; it's a lifelong love affair with the art of storytelling through visuals. Each click of the shutter is an opportunity to weave narratives, to preserve the laughter, the tears, the subtle glances, and the grand celebrations that make life truly extraordinary. In the diverse tapestry of Southern California, I find inspiration in the every day and the extraordinary. From the golden beaches to the urban skylines, my camera is a faithful companion, ready to document the unique stories that unfold against the backdrop of this stunning region. At Anusha Chandra Photography, we specialize in not just freezing moments but crafting visual tales that resonate with emotion. Whether it's a housewarming event, a birthday party,  a family portrait session, a Newborn or a maternity shoot, or any event, our lens is attuned to the nuances that make each occasion special. Our expertise extends beyond photography, embracing the dynamic world of videography to bring your moments to life in motion.<span class="more-links" style="display: none;"><a title="Read More about Anusha Chandra&nbsp;Photography" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDescriptionWeb(this)">Read more</a></span></p>
